
-----title
西安（万年） (出生地)
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='a3a7d2dc212d41f6865cb7bd90bd8f00_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("a3a7d2dc212d41f6865cb7bd90bd8f00");'><span id='a3a7d2dc212d41f6865cb7bd90bd8f00_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=698&endYear=698')">698年</a>　出生。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=699&endYear=707')">699-707年</a>　家境贫寒，早年曾在灞上“躬耕”作品：题灞池二首。独游。王昌龄《郑县宿陶大公馆中赠冯六元二》：“儒有轻王侯，脱略当世务。无何困躬耕，且欲驰永路。”可知诗人家境贫寒，早年曾在灞上“躬耕”。<div id='poem_8734' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_8734' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/8734?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题灞池二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（701年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18440, "盛唐", "王昌龄", "poem_title_8734")'>王昌龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_8734_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_8734'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_8734'>腰镰欲何之，东园刈秋韭。<div id='poem_sentence_0_8734_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_8734'>世事不复论，悲歌和<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_8734", 8734, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>樵叟</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_8734_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_8734'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_8734_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_8735' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_8735' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/8735?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span id='poem_content_8735'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_8735'>开门望长川，薄暮见渔者。<div id='poem_sentence_0_8735_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_8735'>借问<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_8735", 8735, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>白头翁</span>，垂纶几年也。<div id='poem_sentence_1_8735_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_8735'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_8735_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_8692' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_8692' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/8692?labeling=true' target='_blank'>独游</a><span class='authorDate'>（702年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18440, "盛唐", "王昌龄", "poem_title_8692")'>王昌龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_8692_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_8692'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_8692'>林卧情每<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作自）</span>閒，独游景常晏。<div id='poem_sentence_0_8692_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_8692'>时从灞陵下，垂钓往南涧。<div id='poem_sentence_1_8692_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_8692'>手携双鲤鱼，目送千里雁。<div id='poem_sentence_2_8692_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_8692'>悟彼飞<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作非）</span>有适，知此罹忧患。<div id='poem_sentence_3_8692_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_8692'>放之清冷泉，因得省疏慢。<div id='poem_sentence_4_8692_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_8692'>永怀青岑客，回首白云间。<div id='poem_sentence_5_8692_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_8692'>神超物无违<span ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=723&endYear=723')">723年</a>　开元十一年(723)秋冬，返回长安，回到灞上。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=724&endYear=724')">724年</a>　春，旅次盖屋。作品：旅次整厘过韩七别业。<div id='poem_8713' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_8713' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18440, "盛唐", "王昌龄", "poem_title_8713")'>王昌龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_8713_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_8713_0'>① 以下并见《秘府论》引王昌龄《诗格》</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_8713'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_8713'>春烟桑柘林，落日隐荒墅。<div id='poem_sentence_0_8713_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_8713'>泱漭平原夕，清吟久延伫。<div id='poem_sentence_1_8713_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_8713'>故人家于此，招我渔樵所<span class='inlineComment2'>（《格》云：此第五句入作势）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_8713_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_8713'></div><div id='poem_sentence_3_8713_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='63f3c1cdfd384e27abdf7193922abbef_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("63f3c1cdfd384e27abdf7193922abbef");'><span id='63f3c1cdfd384e27abdf7193922abbef_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=726&endYear=726')">726年</a>，29岁</div><div id='63f3c1cdfd384e27abdf7193922abbef' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>王昌龄从西北边塞返回长安，已是开元十四年(726)初。在进士及第之前，曾在石门谷隐居.其谷风景幽美，有溪流，有佛寺。作品：山中别庞十。<div id='poem_8629' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_8629' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/8629?labeling=true' target='_blank'>山中别庞十</a><span class='authorDate'>（726年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: id='poem_sentence_0_8629_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_8629'>散发卧其下，谁知<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_8629", 8629, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>孤隐</span>情。<div id='poem_sentence_1_8629_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_8629'>吟时白<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作碧）</span>云合，钓<span id='poem_sentence_0_8694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_8694'>北风何萧萧，兹夕露为霜。<div id='poem_sentence_1_8694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=727&endYear=727')">727年</a>　自开元十五年(727)至开元二十一年(733)，王昌龄在京城长安任秘书省校书郎。唐于秘书省设秘书郎四员，从六品上；校书郎八人，正九品上，其职掌为典校藏书。本诗及以下各诗，可能作于此期。作品：九日登高。<div id='poem_8627' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_8627' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/8627?labeling=true' target='_blank'>九日登高</a><span class='authorDate'>（727年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span id='poem_sentence_2_8627'>茱萸插鬓花宜寿，翡翠横钗舞作愁。<div id='poem_sentence_2_8627_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_8627'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_8627", 8627, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>谩说</span>陶潜篱下醉，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_8627", 8627, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>何曾</span>得见此风流。<div id='poem_sentence_3_8627_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_8627'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_8627_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=728&endYear=728')">728年</a>　自开元十五年(727)至开元二十一年(734)，王昌龄在京城长安任秘书省校书郎。唐于秘书省设秘书郎四员，从六品上；校书郎八人，正九品上，其职掌为典校藏书。本诗及以下各诗，可能作于此期。作品：甘泉歌。<div id='poem_8566' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_8566' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/8566?labeling=true' target='_blank'>甘泉歌</a><span class='authorDate'>（728年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18440, "盛唐", "王昌龄", "poem_title_8566")'>王昌龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_8566_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_8566'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_8566'>乘舆执玉已登坛，细草沾衣春殿寒。<div id='poem_sentence_0_8566_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_8566'>昨夜云生拜初月，万年甘露水晶盘。<div id='poem_sentence_1_8566_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_8566'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_8566_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=729&endYear=729')">729年</a>　自开元十五年(727)至开元二十一年(735)，王昌龄在京城长安任秘书省校书郎。唐于秘书省设秘书郎四员，从六品上；校书郎八人，正九品上，其职掌为典校藏书。本诗及以下各诗，可能作于此期。作品：萧驸马宅花烛。<span class='inlineComment2'>（据《新唐书·诸帝公主传》：玄宗二十九女，“新昌公主，下嫁萧衡。”《旧唐书·萧嵩传》：“(开元十五年)乃加嵩同中书门下三晶，恩顾莫比。……子衡，尚新昌公主。嵩夫人贺氏人觐拜席，玄宗呼为亲家母，礼仪甚盛。”萧衡官太仆卿、驸马都尉。）</span><div id='poem_8620' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_8620' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/8620?labeling=true' target='_blank'>萧驸马宅花烛</a><span class='authorDate'>（729年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment2'>（花萼楼：《长安志》卷九《唐京城三》：“南内兴庆宫，距外郭城东垣。宫之正门西向曰兴庆门，南曰通阳门，北曰跃龙门，西南隅曰勤政务本楼，其西榜曰花萼相辉楼。”兴庆宫在长安城内兴庆坊，遗址在今西安和平门外咸宁路北兴庆公园，1958年重修了花萼相辉楼。）</span><div id='poem_8650' class='_poem'><div id='poem_sentence_2_8574_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=744&endYear=744')">744年</a>　停留长安。王昌龄自江宁北返后，停留长安一年有余。其间与王玙、李白、王维、王缙、裴迪、岑参等人皆有交往。期间与王维、王缙、裴迪等游青龙寺，彼此唱和。王维等亦有《青龙寺县壁上人兄院集》诗。王维诗序云：“时江宁大兄
持片石，命维序之，诗五韵，座上成。”作品：同王维集青龙寺县壁上人兄院五韵。<div id='poem_8648' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_8648' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/8648?labeling=true' class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_8648'>本来清净所，竹树引幽阴。<div id='poem_sentence_0_8648_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_8648'>檐外含山翠，人间出世心。<div id='poem_sentence_1_8648_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_8648'>圆通无有象，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_8648", 8648, -----title
华阴
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='c91c983dc82e4b4fb4472fd2d364625b_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("c91c983dc82e4b4fb4472fd2d364625b");'><span id='c91c983dc82e4b4fb4472fd2d364625b_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=708&endYear=708')">708年</a>　游历河南、河北。本诗及以下各诗，皆作于此行。作品：小敷谷龙潭祠作。<span class='inlineComment2'>（王昌龄青年时期，也曾像李白那样，  “仗剑去国，辞亲远游”。开元十一年(七二三)之前，他曾游历河南、河北。本诗及以下各诗，皆作于此行。）</span><div id='poem_8656' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_8656' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/8656?labeling=true' class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_8656'>百泉势相荡，巨石皆却立。<div id='poem_sentence_1_8656_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_8656'>跳波沸<span class='link' id='poem_sentence_3_8656'>昏为蛟龙怒<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作窟）</span>，清<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作时）</span>见云雨入。<div id='poem_sentence_3_8656_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_8656'>奔飞振吕梁，忠信亦我习。<div id='poem_sentence_9_8656_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_8656'>波流浸已广，悔吝在所汲。<div -----title
商丘（睢阳）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='e85dcc845c7142a6a6def80bf3de9673_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("e85dcc845c7142a6a6def80bf3de9673");'><span id='e85dcc845c7142a6a6def80bf3de9673_link' class='inlineComment2'>（葛洪《西京杂记》云：‘梁孝王苑中有落猿岩、栖龙岫、雁池、鹤洲、凫岛。诸宫观相连，奇果佳树，瑰禽异兽，靡不毕备。’俗人言梁孝王竹园也。”）</span><div id='poem_8619' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_8619' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/8619?labeling=true' target='_blank'>梁苑</a><span class='authorDate'>（711年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: id='poem_content_8619'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_8619'>梁园秋竹古时烟，城外风悲欲暮天。<div id='poem_sentence_0_8619_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_8619'>万乘旌旗<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_8619", 8619, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>何处</span>在？平台宾客有谁怜。<div id='poem_sentence_1_8619_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_8619'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_8619_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=712&endYear=712')">712年</a>　诗人漫游睢阳(今河南商丘南)之后，曾有南下江南之意，但是没有实现：“渺然江南意，惜与中途违。”于是回访嵩山(今河南登封北)，此诗当作于去嵩山途中。作品：途中作。<div id='poem_8719' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_8719' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/8719?labeling=true' target='_blank'>途中作</a><span class='authorDate'>（712年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18440, "盛唐", "王昌龄", "poem_title_8719")'>王昌龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_8719_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_8719'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_8719'>游人愁岁晏，早起遵王畿。<div id='poem_sentence_0_8719_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_8719'>坠叶吹未晓，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_8719", 8719, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>疏林</span>月微微。<div id='poem_sentence_1_8719_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_8719'>惊禽栖不定，寒兽相因依。<div id='poem_sentence_2_8719_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_8719'>叹此霜露下，复闻鸿雁飞。<div id='poem_sentence_3_8719_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_8719'>渺然江南意，惜与中途违。<div id='poem_sentence_4_8719_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_8719'>羁旅悲<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_8719", 8719, "Clauses/10/Comments/0")'>壮发</span>，别离念征衣。<div id='poem_sentence_5_8719_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_8719'>永图岂劳止，明节期所归。<div id='poem_sentence_6_8719_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_8719'>宁厌楚山曲，无人长掩扉。<div -----title
登封
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='59d70b14c4444538885a47e8de4c84ff_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("59d70b14c4444538885a47e8de4c84ff");'><span id='59d70b14c4444538885a47e8de4c84ff_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=713&endYear=713')">713年</a>　访道求仙。王昌龄《赵十四兄见谢》：  “晚来常读易，顷者欲还嵩。世事何须道，黄精且养蒙。”可知诗人早年曾访道于嵩山。作品：谒焦炼师。<div id='poem_8639' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_8639_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_8639'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_8639'>中峰青苔壁，一点云生时。<div id='poem_sentence_3_8639'>拜受长年药，翩翻西海期。<div id='poem_sentence_3_8639_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_8639'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_8639_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=714&endYear=714')">714年</a>　在嵩山学道不成，乃有北上太行之意。诗人离开嵩山、北上太行山前夕就道士问周易，赋诗。作品：就道士问周易参同契。<div id='poem_8724' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_8724' class='poemTitle class='poemContent' id='poem_content_8724'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_8724'>仙人骑白鹿，发短耳何长。<div id='poem_sentence_0_8724_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_8724'>时余采菖蒲，忽见嵩之阳。<div id='poem_sentence_1_8724_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_8724'>稽首求丹经，乃出怀中方。<div id='poem_sentence_2_8724_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_8724'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_8724", 8724, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>披读</span>了不悟，归来问嵇康。<div id='poem_sentence_3_8724_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_8724'>嗟余无<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_8724", 8724, "Clauses/8/Comments/0")'>道骨</span>，发我入太行。<div id='poem_sentence_4_8724_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' 邯郸

-----title
太原
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='6a8dfa263f2f4d9db390bf322dedbeb9_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("6a8dfa263f2f4d9db390bf322dedbeb9");'><span id='6a8dfa263f2f4d9db390bf322dedbeb9_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=722&endYear=723')">722-723年</a>，25-26岁</div><div id='6a8dfa263f2f4d9db390bf322dedbeb9' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=722&endYear=722')">722年</a>　开元十一年(723)前，王昌龄曾漫游河南、河北，今又来到河东，客居并州(今山西太原)、潞州(今山西长治)，当与唐玄宗幸河东有关。此诗是一种颂德体，或为上献而作。作品：驾幸河东。<div id='poem_8634' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_8634' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/8634?labeling=true' target='_blank'>驾幸河东</a><span class='authorDate'>（722年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18440, "盛唐", "王昌龄", "poem_title_8634")'>王昌龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_8634_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_8634'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_8634'>晋水千庐合，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_8634", 8634, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>汾桥</span>万国从。<div id='poem_sentence_0_8634_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_8634'>开唐<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_8634", 8634, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>天业</span>盛，入沛<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_8634", 8634, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>圣恩</span>浓。<div id='poem_sentence_1_8634_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_8634'>下辇回三象，题碑任六龙。<div id='poem_sentence_2_8634_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_8634'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_8634", 8634, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>睿明</span>悬日月，千岁<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作载）</span>此时逢。<div id='poem_sentence_3_8634_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_8634'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_8634_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=723&endYear=723')">723年</a>　客居太原，寒食节赋诗。作品：寒食即事。<div id='poem_8640' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_8640' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a -----title
大荔（河西）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='bc7fc9825e3f46748caad06b45449a78_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("bc7fc9825e3f46748caad06b45449a78");'><span id='bc7fc9825e3f46748caad06b45449a78_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=723&endYear=723')">723年</a>，26岁</div><div id='bc7fc9825e3f46748caad06b45449a78' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=723&endYear=723')">723年</a>　诗人客居潞州以后，曾至同州(今陕西大荔)上书作刺史的伯父(《上同州使君伯》)，但没有得到引荐和任用，便急于返长安。作品：沙苑南渡头。<div id='poem_8682' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_8682' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/8682?labeling=true' target='_blank'>沙苑南渡头</a><span class='authorDate'>（723年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18440, "盛唐", "王昌龄", "poem_title_8682")'>王昌龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_8682_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_8682'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_8682'>秋雾连云白，归心浦溆悬。<div id='poem_sentence_0_8682_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_8682'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_8682", 8682, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>津人</span>空守缆，村馆复临川。<div id='poem_sentence_1_8682_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_8682'>篷<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作峰）</span>隔<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_8682", 8682, "Clauses/4/Comments/1")'>苍茫</span>雨，波连<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作通）</span>演漾田。<div id='poem_sentence_2_8682_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_8682'>孤舟未得济，入梦在何年。<div id='poem_sentence_3_8682_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_8682'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_8682_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

id='poem_sentence_12_8665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_8665'>禽兽悲不去，路傍谁忍看。<div id='poem_sentence_13_8665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' -----title
固原（萧关）
-----detail

0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>漫游河西、陇右边塞。在泾州、萧关、白草原都写过诗。作品：旅望。塞下曲四首。从军行七首。<div id='poem_8642' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_8642' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/8642?labeling=true' class='inlineComment2'>（一作桑树间）</span>，八月萧关道。<div id='poem_sentence_0_8642_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_8642'>出塞入塞寒<span -----title
洛阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='c4366d265d444c5d9b137eea1f1090a6_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("c4366d265d444c5d9b137eea1f1090a6");'><span id='c4366d265d444c5d9b137eea1f1090a6_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=727&endYear=727')">727年</a>，30岁</div><div id='c4366d265d444c5d9b137eea1f1090a6' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=727&endYear=727')">727年</a>　开元十五年(727)，中进土，授秘书省校书郎。此次考试在东都洛阳城举行。顾况《监察御史储公集序》：“开元十四年，严黄门知考功，以鲁国储公进士高第，与崔国辅员外、綦毋潜著作同时；其明年，擢第常建少府、王龙标昌龄。此数人皆当时之秀。”作品：放歌行。<div id='poem_8687' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_8687' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/8687?labeling=true' target='_blank'>放歌行<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作相和歌辞 放歌行）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（727年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18440, "盛唐", "王昌龄", "poem_title_8687")'>王昌龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_8687_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_8687'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(3177, "poem_allusion_8687")'>负薪裘</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_8687_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_8687'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_8687'>南渡<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作望）</span>洛阳津，西望<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_8687", 8687, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>十二楼</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_8687_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_8687'>明堂坐天子，月朔朝诸侯。<div id='poem_sentence_1_8687_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_8687'>清乐动千门，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_8687", 8687, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>皇风</span>被九州。<div id='poem_sentence_2_8687_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_8687'>庆云从东来<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作出）</span>，泱漭抱日流。<div id='poem_sentence_3_8687_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_8687'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_8687", 8687, "Clauses/8/Comments/0")'>升平</span>贵论道，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_8687", 8687, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>文墨</span>将何求？<div id='poem_sentence_4_8687_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_8687'>有诏徵<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_8687", 8687, "Clauses/10/Comments/0")'>草泽</span>，微诚将献谋<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作献谋猷）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_5_8687_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_8687'>冠冕如星罗，拜揖曹与周。<div id='poem_sentence_6_8687_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_8687'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_8687", 8687, "Clauses/14/Comments/1")'>望尘</span>非吾<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作君）</span>事，入赋<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作职）</span>且迟留。<div id='poem_sentence_7_8687_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_8687'>幸蒙国士识，因脱<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(3177, "poem_sentence_8_8687")'>负薪裘</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_8_8687_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_8687'>今者放歌行，以慰梁甫愁。<div id='poem_sentence_9_8687_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_8687'>但营数斗禄，奉养每<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_8687", 8687, "Clauses/21/Comments/0")'>丰羞</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_10_8687_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_8687'>若<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作愿）</span>得金膏遂，飞云亦何<span -----title
蓝田
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='f610586658ff46c3a2c574ee989614d9_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("f610586658ff46c3a2c574ee989614d9");'><span id='f610586658ff46c3a2c574ee989614d9_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=732&endYear=732')">732年</a>，35岁</div><div id='f610586658ff46c3a2c574ee989614d9' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>自开元十五年(727)至开元二十一年(739)，王昌龄在京城长安任秘书省校书郎。唐于秘书省设秘书郎四员，从六品上；校书郎八人，正九品上，其职掌为典校藏书。本诗及以下各诗，可能作于此期。作品：风凉原上作。<span class='inlineComment2'>（：《长安志》卷一六《蓝田县》：“风凉原，在县西南四十五里，南接石门山，北入万年县界。《遁甲开山图》曰：骊山之西川有阜名曰风凉原，亦雍州之福地，即硗山之阴也。”）</span><div id='poem_8663' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_8663' class='poemTitle -----title
华县（郑县）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='a0cf1561e1cf4cf69233e5a977a2ec1c_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("a0cf1561e1cf4cf69233e5a977a2ec1c");'><span id='a0cf1561e1cf4cf69233e5a977a2ec1c_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=732&endYear=732')">732年</a>，35岁</div><div id='a0cf1561e1cf4cf69233e5a977a2ec1c' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=732&endYear=732')">732年</a>　因事去郑县，宿于朋友家中为赠友人而作。作品：郑县宿陶大公馆中赠冯六元二。<span class='inlineComment2'>（陶大：陶翰。顾况轩乙部员外郎陶氏集序》：“唐词臣姓陶氏，开元十八年进士上第。”据《登科记考》云，开元十九年(731)王昌龄与陶翰又同中博学宏词科。陶敏《全唐诗人名考证》引《宝刻丛编》卷一O华州：“《唐华岳真君碑》，唐华阴丞陶翰撰，韦胜书。玄宗开元十九年，加五岳神号曰真君，初建祠宇，立此碑(《集古录目》)。”知开元二十年左右陶翰在华州，华阴丞或为郑县丞之误。陶翰官至礼部员外郎。《全唐诗》存其诗一卷。冯六：不详。元二：不详。）</span><div id='poem_8688' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_8688' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/8688?labeling=true' target='_blank'>郑县宿陶太公馆中赠冯六元二</a><span class='authorDate'>（732年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18440, "盛唐", "王昌龄", "poem_title_8688")'>王昌龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_8688_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_8688'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(299, "poem_allusion_8688")'>张范善终始</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_8688_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_8688'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_8688'>儒有轻王侯，脱略当世务<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作誉）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_8688_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_8688'>本家蓝田下<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作溪中）</span>，非为<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_8688", 8688, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>渔弋</span>故。<div id='poem_sentence_1_8688_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_8688'>无何<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作才）</span>困躬耕，且欲驰永路。<div id='poem_sentence_5_8688'>云龙未相感，干谒亦已屡。<div id='poem_sentence_5_8688_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_8688'>子为黄绶羁，余忝蓬山顾。<div "Clauses/14/Comments/0")'>京门</span>望西岳，百里见郊树。<div id='poem_sentence_7_8688_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_8688'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_8688", 8688, "Clauses/16/Comments/1")'>飞雨</span>祠上<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作下）</span>来，霭然关中暮。<div id='poem_sentence_8_8688_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_8688'>驱车郑城宿，秉烛论<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_8688", 8688, "Clauses/19/Comments/0")'>往素</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_12_8688_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_8688'>拂衣易为高，沦迹难有趣。<div id='poem_sentence_13_8688_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' -----title
伊川（伊阙）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='14b619f2211f4abbba738577079002a6_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("14b619f2211f4abbba738577079002a6");'><span id='14b619f2211f4abbba738577079002a6_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=739&endYear=739')">739年</a>，42岁</div><div id='14b619f2211f4abbba738577079002a6' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>途径伊阙。因罪由汜水贬岭南，途径伊水，作诗。作品：存句：“得罪由己招，本性易然诺。”（《见谴至伊水》）<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在伊阙。诗人由汜水贬岭南，由伊水、洛水南下伊
阙，有此留赠之作。作品：留别伊阙张少府郭大都尉。<div id='poem_8715' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_8715' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/8715?labeling=true' target='_blank'>留别伊阙张少府郭大都尉</a><span -----title
襄阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='eb99b6b685ab4fc48fafda50ef19cadb_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("eb99b6b685ab4fc48fafda50ef19cadb");'><span id='eb99b6b685ab4fc48fafda50ef19cadb_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=739&endYear=739')">739年</a>，42岁</div><div id='eb99b6b685ab4fc48fafda50ef19cadb' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=739&endYear=739')">739年</a>　秋，贬谪岭南，途径襄阳，拜访孟浩然。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='ea1dd5fe2c324c2ca69959f4e4af1b9b_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("ea1dd5fe2c324c2ca69959f4e4af1b9b");'><span id='ea1dd5fe2c324c2ca69959f4e4af1b9b_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=740&endYear=740')">740年</a>，43岁</div><div id='ea1dd5fe2c324c2ca69959f4e4af1b9b' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=740&endYear=740')">740年</a>　翌年北归，游襄阳，访孟浩然。时浩然疾疹且逾，食鲜疾动，遂致暴卒。<br /></div>

-----title
长沙
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='155d95bcb42a434b8776d825a1091a32_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("155d95bcb42a434b8776d825a1091a32");'><span id='155d95bcb42a434b8776d825a1091a32_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=739&endYear=739')">739年</a>，42岁</div><div id='155d95bcb42a434b8776d825a1091a32' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; -----title
郴州
-----detail

onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_8678", 8678, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>罍觞</span>且终宴，功业曾<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作会）</span>未了。<div id='poem_sentence_1_8678_comment'></div></div><div -----title
南陵（宣城）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='c4cae83117204aaa8f230722a3b59e8e_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("c4cae83117204aaa8f230722a3b59e8e");'><span id='c4cae83117204aaa8f230722a3b59e8e_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=749&endYear=749')">749年</a>，52岁</div><div id='c4cae83117204aaa8f230722a3b59e8e' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>秋，贬为龙标尉王昌龄沿长江而上，至鄂措(今湖北武昌)而南下洞庭湖，经沉江至龙标。至南陵有诗寄友人皇甫岳，王诗残句：“昨从金陵邑。远访沉淫滨。”作品：至南陵答皇甫岳。<div id='poem_8568' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_8568' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/8568?labeling=true' target='_blank'>至南陵答皇甫岳</a><span class='authorDate'>（749年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18440, "盛唐", "王昌龄", "poem_title_8568")'>王昌龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_8568_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_8568'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_8568'>与君同病复漂沦，昨夜宣城别故人。<div id='poem_sentence_0_8568_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_8568'>明主恩深非岁久，长江还共五溪滨。<div id='poem_sentence_1_8568_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_8568'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_8568_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>秋，贬谪龙标途中，于西江作诗寄从弟王越。作品：西江寄越弟。<div id='poem_8569' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_8569' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/8569?labeling=true' target='_blank'>西江寄越弟</a><span class='authorDate'>（749年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 盛唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18440, "盛唐", "王昌龄", "poem_title_8569")'>王昌龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_8569_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_8569'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_8569'>南浦逢君岭外还，沅溪更远洞庭山。<div id='poem_sentence_0_8569_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_8569'>尧时恩泽如春雨，梦里相逢同入关。<div id='poem_sentence_1_8569_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_8569'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_8569_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title

id='poem_sentence_3_8730_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_8730'>将军铁骢汗血流，深入匈奴战未休。<div id='poem_sentence_4_8730_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_8730'>黄旗一点兵马收，乱杀胡人积如丘。<div id='poem_sentence_5_8730_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_8730'>疮病驱来配<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作役）</span>边州，仍披<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_8730", 8730, "Clauses/13/Comments/0")'>漠北</span>羔羊裘。<div id='poem_sentence_6_8730_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_8730'>颜色<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_8730", 8730, id='poem_sentence_8_8730_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_8730'>或有强壮能咿嚘，意说被他边将雠。<div id='poem_sentence_9_8730_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_8730'>五世属藩汉主留，碧毛毡帐河曲游。<div id='poem_sentence_10_8730_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_8730'>橐驼五万部落稠，敕赐飞凤金兜鍪。<div id='poem_sentence_11_8730_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_8730'>为君百战如过筹，静扫阴山无鸟投。<div id='poem_sentence_12_8730_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_8730'>家藏铁券特承优，黄金千<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作百）</span>斤不称求。<div id='poem_sentence_13_8730_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_8730'><span -----title
洪江（龙标）

id='poem_sentence_0_8684_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_8684'>天下尽兵甲，豺狼满中原。<div id='poem_sentence_1_8684_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_8684'>明夷方<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_8684", 8684, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>遘患</span>，顾我徒崩奔。<div id='poem_sentence_2_8684_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_8684'>自惭<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_8684", 8684, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>菲薄</span>才，误蒙国士恩。<div id='poem_sentence_3_8684_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_8684'>位重任亦重，时危志弥敦。<div id='poem_sentence_4_8684_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_8684'>西北未及终，东南不可吞。<div id='poem_sentence_5_8684_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_8684'>进则耻保躬，退乃为<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(1817, "poem_sentence_6_8684")'>触藩</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_6_8684_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_8684'>叹息嵩山老，而后知其尊<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_7_8684_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_8684'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_8684_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_8684'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_7_8684_0'>⑴ 本集《咏史》云：“荷畚至洛阳，胡马屯北门。天下裂其土，豺狼满中原。明夷方济世，敛翼黄埃昏。披云见龙颜，始蒙国士恩。位重谋亦深，所举无遗奔。长策寄临终，东南不可吞。贤智苟有时，贫贱安所论。惟然嵩山老，而后知我言。”</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_8684_comment'></div></div><br /></div>
